# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
2 ^h7npe7eZ

If x is in radians, we can see from the graph that as x approaches 0, the two graphs are approximately the same, i.e sinx ≈ x ^URDp9DCq

If x was in degrees however, then we can see this is not the case. ^L7QWXmRl

When θ is small and measured in radians:
sin θ ≈ θ
tan θ ≈ θ
cos θ ≈ 1 - θ /2 ^5d4NMGyT

There is a higher percentage uncertainty with 0.75rad compared to 0.244rad, due to angles getting increasingly similar the closer they are to 0. ^vzaV47O5
